## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Domain Lineage: Envoy xDS Configuration Discovery Service Flow

## Your Task

Trace how an xDS configuration update flows from the control plane to Envoy's data plane. Find: 1. In `envoyproxy/go-control-plane`: the Go source files that define the `DiscoveryRequest` and `DiscoveryResponse` types and the `StreamAggregatedResources` gRPC handler. 2. In `envoyproxy/data-plane-api`: the `.proto` files that define the `AggregatedDiscoveryService` and `DeltaDiscoveryService` RPCs. 3. In `envoyproxy/envoy`: the C++ source files under `source/common/config/` that implement the xDS client subscription logic (look for `GrpcSubscriptionImpl` or `XdsResourceDelegate`). Report the repo, file path, and key type/service name for each hop in the configuration delivery chain.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:

- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

## Key Findings

### 1. **Protocol Definition** (Data Plane API)
- **`envoy/api/v2/discovery.proto`** and **`envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.proto`**: Define core message types (DiscoveryRequest, DiscoveryResponse, DeltaDiscoveryRequest, DeltaDiscoveryResponse)
- **`envoy/service/discovery/v2/ads.proto`** and **`envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads.proto`**: Define the AggregatedDiscoveryService with StreamAggregatedResources and DeltaAggregatedResources RPCs

### 2. **Control Plane Server** (Go Control Plane)
- **`pkg/server/v3/server.go`**: Implements StreamAggregatedResources() handler that receives DiscoveryRequest and sends DiscoveryResponse
- **`envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads_grpc.pb.go`**: Generated gRPC service stubs

### 3. **Data Plane Client** (Envoy C++)
- **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h`/`.cc`**: GrpcSubscriptionImpl class that manages subscriptions and handles config updates
- **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h`**: GrpcMuxImpl multiplexer for batching multiple resource types on a single ADS stream
- **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h`**: Low-level gRPC stream management
- **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h`** and **`delta_subscription_state.h`**: State management for different xDS modes

### 4. **Configuration Update Flow**
The answer.json includes an 8-step chain documenting how a configuration update flows from control plane to Envoy, including multiplexing, version tracking, and ACK/NACK semantics.

plane through a gRPC streaming mechanism:\\n\\n## 1. Protocol Definition (Data Plane API)\\n\\nThe control plane and data plane communication is defined in protobuf files in the `data-plane-api` repository. The core message types are defined in `envoy/api/v2/discovery.proto` (legacy v2) and `envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.proto` (current v3):\\n- **DiscoveryRequest**: Sent by Envoy to request resources (includes node info, resource names, version info, type_url)\\n- **DiscoveryResponse**: Sent by the control plane with versioned resources, nonce for ACK/NACK\\n- **DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response**: Incremental variants for efficient partial updates\\n\\nThe **AggregatedDiscoveryService** is defined in `envoy/service/discovery/v2/ads.proto` (v2) and `envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads.proto` (v3), which provides two gRPC RPCs:\\n- **StreamAggregatedResources**: Bidirectional stream for state-of-the-world xDS\\n- **DeltaAggregatedResources**: Bidirectional stream for incremental xDS updates\\n\\n## 2. Control Plane Server (Go Control Plane)\\n\\nThe `go-control-plane` repository provides the server-side implementation:\\n- **envoy/api/v2/discovery.pb.go** and **envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.pb.go**: Generated Go protocol buffer bindings\\n- **envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads_grpc.pb.go**: Generated gRPC service stubs with AggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer interface\\n- **pkg/server/v3/server.go**: The actual server implementation that:\\n  - Implements **StreamAggregatedResources()**: Handles incoming gRPC streams from Envoy clients\\n  - Calls **StreamHandler()**: Routes requests to the appropriate xDS handler (sotw, delta, or rest)\\n  - Sends DiscoveryResponse messages back to clients\\n\\n## 3. Data Plane Client (Envoy C++)\\n\\nEnvoy's data plane uses these key components in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/`:\\n\\n**GrpcSubscriptionImpl** (`grpc_subscription_impl.h`/`.cc`):\\n- Wraps the generic GrpcMux with configuration-specific callbacks\\n- **start()**: Initiates subscription by registering a watch on the GrpcMux\\n- **updateResourceInterest()**: Updates the set of subscribed resources\\n- **onConfigUpdate()**: Callback invoked when the control plane sends DiscoveryResponse\\n- Manages per-resource-type version tracking and statistics\\n\\n**GrpcMuxImpl** (`xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h`):\\n- Multiplexes multiple resource types (LDS, CDS, RDS, EDS) onto a single ADS gRPC stream\\n- Maintains a WatchMap tracking all subscribed resources\\n- Batches subscription requests and ACKs them with appropriate nonces\\n- Manages connection state and failover\\n\\n**GrpcStream** (`grpc_stream.h`):\\n- Low-level gRPC stream management\\n- Sends DiscoveryRequest messages (or DeltaDiscoveryRequest for delta xDS)\\n- Receives DiscoveryResponse (or DeltaDiscoveryResponse)\\n- Handles gRPC reconnection and rate limiting\\n\\n**Subscription State Management** (`xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h`, `xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h`):\\n- **SotwSubscriptionState**: Tracks server-sent resources for state-of-the-world xDS\\n- **DeltaSubscriptionState**: Tracks per-resource versions for incremental updates\\n- Generates appropriate DiscoveryRequest messages based on subscriptions and ACKs\\n\\n## Configuration Update Flow\\n\\n1. Envoy subsystems (LDS, CDS, RDS, EDS) create GrpcSubscriptionImpl instances\\n2. When subscription starts, GrpcSubscriptionImpl.start() registers a watch with GrpcMux\\n3. GrpcMux batches all subscriptions and sends an initial DiscoveryRequest over the ADS stream\\n4. Control plane's StreamAggregatedResources() handler (in go-control-plane) receives the request\\n5. Server matches the requested resources and sends back a DiscoveryResponse with versioned resources\\n6. GrpcStream receives the DiscoveryResponse\\n7. Subscription state machine unmarshals the resources and calls GrpcSubscriptionImpl.onConfigUpdate()\\n8. The callback propagates configuration to the target subsystem (e.g., RouteConfigProvider)\\n9. Envoy ACKs by sending a new DiscoveryRequest with the response nonce and matching version_info\\n10. Control plane uses the nonce to correlate the ACK and track configuration acceptance\\n\\nThe mux design allows Envoy to receive multiple resource types over a single gRPC stream while maintaining independent version tracking and ACK/NACK semantics per resource type.\"\n}\n",

Protocol Definition (Data Plane API)\\n\\nThe control plane and data plane communication is defined in protobuf files in the `data-plane-api` repository. The core message types are defined in `envoy/api/v2/discovery.proto` (legacy v2) and `envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.proto` (current v3):\\n- **DiscoveryRequest**: Sent by Envoy to request resources (includes node info, resource names, version info, type_url)\\n- **DiscoveryResponse**: Sent by the control plane with versioned resources, nonce for ACK/NACK\\n- **DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response**: Incremental variants for efficient partial updates\\n\\nThe **AggregatedDiscoveryService** is defined in `envoy/service/discovery/v2/ads.proto` (v2) and `envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads.proto` (v3), which provides two gRPC RPCs:\\n- **StreamAggregatedResources**: Bidirectional stream for state-of-the-world xDS\\n- **DeltaAggregatedResources**: Bidirectional stream for incremental xDS updates\\n\\n## 2. Control Plane Server (Go Control Plane)\\n\\nThe `go-control-plane` repository provides the server-side implementation:\\n- **envoy/api/v2/discovery.pb.go** and **envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.pb.go**: Generated Go protocol buffer bindings\\n- **envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads_grpc.pb.go**: Generated gRPC service stubs with AggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer interface\\n- **pkg/server/v3/server.go**: The actual server implementation that:\\n  - Implements **StreamAggregatedResources()**: Handles incoming gRPC streams from Envoy clients\\n  - Calls **StreamHandler()**: Routes requests to the appropriate xDS handler (sotw, delta, or rest)\\n  - Sends DiscoveryResponse messages back to clients\\n\\n## 3. Data Plane Client (Envoy C++)\\n\\nEnvoy's data plane uses these key components in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/`:\\n\\n**GrpcSubscriptionImpl** (`grpc_subscription_impl.h`/`.cc`):\\n- Wraps the generic GrpcMux with configuration-specific callbacks\\n- **start()**: Initiates subscription by registering a watch on the GrpcMux\\n- **updateResourceInterest()**: Updates the set of subscribed resources\\n- **onConfigUpdate()**: Callback invoked when the control plane sends DiscoveryResponse\\n- Manages per-resource-type version tracking and statistics\\n\\n**GrpcMuxImpl** (`xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h`):\\n- Multiplexes multiple resource types (LDS, CDS, RDS, EDS) onto a single ADS gRPC stream\\n- Maintains a WatchMap tracking all subscribed resources\\n- Batches subscription requests and ACKs them with appropriate nonces\\n- Manages connection state and failover\\n\\n**GrpcStream** (`grpc_stream.h`):\\n- Low-level gRPC stream management\\n- Sends DiscoveryRequest messages (or DeltaDiscoveryRequest for delta xDS)\\n- Receives DiscoveryResponse (or DeltaDiscoveryResponse)\\n- Handles gRPC reconnection and rate limiting\\n\\n**Subscription State Management** (`xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h`, `xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h`):\\n- **SotwSubscriptionState**: Tracks server-sent resources for state-of-the-world xDS\\n- **DeltaSubscriptionState**: Tracks per-resource versions for incremental updates\\n- Generates appropriate DiscoveryRequest messages based on subscriptions and ACKs\\n\\n## Configuration Update Flow\\n\\n1. Envoy subsystems (LDS, CDS, RDS, EDS) create GrpcSubscriptionImpl instances\\n2. When subscription starts, GrpcSubscriptionImpl.start() registers a watch with GrpcMux\\n3. GrpcMux batches all subscriptions and sends an initial DiscoveryRequest over the ADS stream\\n4. Control plane's StreamAggregatedResources() handler (in go-control-plane) receives the request\\n5. Server matches the requested resources and sends back a DiscoveryResponse with versioned resources\\n6. GrpcStream receives the DiscoveryResponse\\n7. Subscription state machine unmarshals the resources and calls GrpcSubscriptionImpl.onConfigUpdate()\\n8. The callback propagates configuration to the target subsystem (e.g., RouteConfigProvider)\\n9. Envoy ACKs by sending a new DiscoveryRequest with the response nonce and matching version_info\\n10. Control plane uses the nonce to correlate the ACK and track configuration acceptance\\n\\nThe mux design allows Envoy to receive multiple resource types over a single gRPC stream while maintaining independent version tracking and ACK/NACK semantics per resource type.\"\n}\n",
